Gu Changming remained silent, then nodded and said, “If you’re right, Senior Brother, I should be similar to you. To be honest, if you hadn’t mentioned it today, I would have thought my spiritual realm had fallen ill.”

This wasn’t just to comfort Gu Changming; Fang Yuan had inquired about this with System 120.

System 120 replied, “No, host, Gu Changming is still in a period of burgeoning fortune. And although you, host, have become the new Child of this World, his fortune is still considerable.”

System 120 also stated that it was the fluctuations generated by Gu Changming’s burgeoning fortune and his contact with you, host, that awakened me.

“However, host, you are far more advanced than a Child of Fortune. You are the Child of the World.”

Gu Changming’s status was only temporary, a product of the times. But Fang Yuan’s position is permanent and will not change with time.

Just like a subject and an emperor, no matter how much power and ability a subject has, subjects will change with time, while an emperor, as long as he exists, will not fall.

Gu Changming continued to ask,

"Then those two people yesterday—"

"Assassins sent by someone to target me. They were somewhat capable, but I've already dealt with them."

"Assassins!"

Hearing this, Gu Changming was still startled. After all, how could such things exist in the early stages of his novel?

But Fang Yuan's next words reassured Gu Changming.

"They've been dealt with."

"You know, I'm not joking. I told you before that you had the ability to believe in yourself because I felt the same way I did, and later I got some clues about this."

He broke through right after the attack.

Because System 120 woke up after the attack.

This wasn't exactly lying to Gu Changming; Fang Yuan would have known once System 120 woke up.

"When did it start?"

"More than ten years ago, I think." Fang Yuan said this without blinking. "There's very little information; most of it I found myself."

Gu Changming looked at him for a while.

Fang Yuan met his gaze without looking away.

This was the part of him that impressed Gu Changming the most. It wasn't that he didn't lie—he could lie without batting an eye. It was that when he was facing you, whether he was telling the truth or a lie, he wouldn't give himself away.

"Alright, don't worry too much."

Gu Changming silently repeated these four words three times in his mind, each time with a different tone. The first time was shock, the second was doubt, and the third was—well, whatever his senior brother said, went ahead.

He took a deep breath, suppressing the surging questions.

If his senior brother said he was investigating, then he was investigating. If his senior brother said it was a spiritual energy revival, then it was a spiritual energy revival.

There was no need to ask further.

He trusted Fang Yuan.

"...I'm going to train." Gu Changming turned, picked up his gym bag from the sofa, and walked steadily to the door. He changed his shoes, opened the door, and closed it. The whole movement was fluid, but Fang Yuan seemed to be controlling it mechanically.

It seems this had a significant impact on Gu Changming.

The footsteps faded into the distance.

"I wonder if I'll ever be able to cultivate immortality."

Hearing Gu Changming's mutterings, Fang Yuan leaned back on the sofa, a slight smile playing on his lips.

"Yes, there will be bread, there will be milk."

"Did he believe it?"

The 120 emergency number sounded in his mind.

"Barely, I guess," Fang Yuan answered in his heart.

Then the 120 completely let go.

"Hey, hey, is this the Chosen One?" The small white ball bounced twice in Fang Yuan's consciousness, its golden edges shimmering. "It looks pretty much the same as you, host."

It jumped to the left of Fang Yuan's field of vision.

"Not even as good-looking as the host."

Then it jumped back to the center.

“But his expression just now was so funny! He was clearly thinking, ‘This is ridiculous!’ but he was forcing himself to stay composed. Ugh, it cracked me up! You humans are really good at fooling yourselves!”

Fang Yuan: “…Weren’t you quite serious just now?”

“That’s different!” 120 said confidently, its voice still childish, carrying the excitement of finally being able to speak after holding it in for so long.

“That was signing a contract! Formal! Of course, I had to be serious. If I were joking around, wouldn’t you think I’m unreliable, host? Wouldn’t you think, ‘Ugh, this system is so unserious, I don’t want to sign a contract with you’—I’d be worried to death, okay!”

It spun around in Fang Yuan’s consciousness space, a faint golden ripple appearing on the surface of its white sphere.

“And I slept for seventeen years! Seventeen years! Even though it felt like a nap to me, seventeen years of nobody talking to me! Do you know what that feels like? It's like waking up from a nap and finding everyone in the world gone, leaving you all alone, and having to pretend you're calm—that's the feeling!”

Fang Yuan was silent for a moment.

“Well, thanks for your hard work, 120.”

It was quiet for two seconds.

Then it lit up again.

“But it’s okay! I’m back now!” The little ball started bouncing again, “And we got promoted! Promoted! Promoted! Host, you know? We went from being employees to partners! Although we’re still nominally affiliated with the system space, we’re actually doing everything ourselves!”

“How exactly?”

System 120 cleared its throat—even though it didn’t have a throat at all—and began its report. Its voice returned to its childish but clear tone, like a child eager to report what happened at school that day.

"First, our status and authority have been elevated. Before, we were employees, with leaders above us, tasks assigned, and profits based on commissions. Now it's different! After merging with the world's will, we've become—how should I put it—like two employees in a large company suddenly discovering they hold the company's core technology patents, and then starting our own business. We may not say it, but we can use the parent company's resources, and we make our own decisions."

"Second, the profit-sharing has changed!" 120's voice rose noticeably. "60/40! 60/40, Host! We get 60%, they get 40%! 60% goes to us, used for the construction and development of this world. 40% goes to the system space, as a channel fee and service fee—well, it's basically a brand franchise fee. Compared to the previous profit-sharing ratio for employees, this is like a windfall!"

The little ball bounced excitedly in Fang Yuan's consciousness space, like an overinflated balloon.

"Third—" 120's voice suddenly lowered, taking on a mysterious tone, "Host, we can dig up that huge world heritage you possess."

Fang Yuan's eyes flickered.

“We couldn’t dig before because we didn’t have the authority or the tools. It’s like having a piece of land, knowing there’s oil buried underneath, but you don’t have the drilling equipment, and the extraction rights haven’t been approved. Now it’s different! We ourselves are the approvers of the extraction rights! As long as we accumulate enough initial capital—that is, we’ll do a few tasks first to accumulate resources—we can start digging into those ‘seeds’ at the bottom of your consciousness.”

120’s voice grew increasingly excited.

“Then, what I just told Gu Changming about the ‘spiritual energy revival’—”

“I said it.” Fang Yuan corrected it.

“Okay, you said it, host—but then it will be real! A real spiritual energy revival! A real world upgrade! You, host, will be the anchor and source of this world’s extraordinary system! Think about it, a world changes because of you, all awakened beings, all extraordinary powers, can trace their origins back to you—wow, what a grand scale, what a vision!”

Fang Yuan didn’t respond immediately.

He sat on the sofa, the morning light having moved to the edge of the coffee table. The water in the glass was no longer sloshing, as still as a small mirror.

“120,” he said.

“Hmm?”

“Where are my parents?”

System 120’s jump stopped.

Although Fang Yuan was adopted by Fang Chenxu and the others, they treated him with their whole hearts. People say that even humans aren’t plants or trees, how can they be without feelings? Fang Yuan, though plant-like, also had emotions.

The small ball hovered in the center of the consciousness space, its surface light slightly diminishing, becoming softer. Like a child who had just been running wildly suddenly stopped by an adult, it quieted down and looked intently at the adult’s face.

“The Divine Kingdom… the Divine Kingdom is still too far away. We’ve just started, talking about that is unrealistic.” 120 seemed to be counting on its fingers, “But space is possible. As long as we work hard, save up, and conserve—after a few missions, we should have the ability to create a secondary space.”

The small ball floated forward a little.

“When Mr. and Mrs. Fang's lives are nearing their end, we can let them go in first. Not for immortality, not for stagnation, just a… a place where they can stay. Once the divine kingdom is truly built, we can bring them over.”

It paused.

“That way, they can stay with the host forever.”

Fang Yuan's fingers tightened slightly.

The sunlight outside the window shone warmly on the back of his hand.

Fang Yuan fell silent.

The ambulance didn't urge him; it simply hung there quietly, its surface glowing and dimming, as if breathing with him.

“This matter,” Fang Yuan finally spoke, his voice low, “must be known by them.”

Fang Yuan looked up at the window. The leaves of the pothos on the windowsill glowed a translucent green in the sunlight, the veins clearly visible.

“Life and death, reincarnation,” he said, “shouldn't be decided by me for them. Life shouldn't be desecrated by me. No one can control another's life—even if that person is my parents.”

Fang Yuan's fingers slowly loosened.

“If they’re willing, I’ll do my best. If they’re not…”

He didn’t finish.

System 120 gently touched the edge of his consciousness, like a kitten rubbing its head against someone’s hand.

System 120 gently touched the edge of his consciousness, like a kitten rubbing its head against someone’s hand.

“The host is right,” the little ball’s voice was soft. “The meaning of life cannot be arbitrarily altered. I fully support the host’s decision.”

A few seconds of silence.

Then 120 suddenly sprang up with a “whoosh,” like a cat whose tail had been stepped on.

“Oops! I almost forgot the important thing after talking so much!”

The little ball hurriedly spun around in the consciousness space.

"I need to go back to the space! We just renewed the contract, so I need to report it. I also need to check the task list to see if there's anything suitable for us right now. Host, your situation is special—you have a large world heritage site to excavate, and you're also bound to the rules of this world. Ordinary tasks might not be suitable; we need to find something that allows us to accumulate resources and excavate heritage simultaneously—"

It muttered to itself as it spun around, making Fang Yuan a little dizzy.

“But don’t worry, host!” 120 suddenly stopped, a golden light illuminating the surface of the sphere. “This time I won’t disappear. I’ve left a wisp of my consciousness here with you, like…like an extension number! Yes, an extension number! Call me anytime you need me. My main body is busy in this space, but my extension is always here!”

Deep within Fang Yuan’s consciousness, a certain place flickered slightly. Very faintly, like a small lamp being lit in a darkroom.

“Just like before,” he said.

“Hmm!” 120’s voice carried a hint of amusement. “Just like before. Unchanged intentions, the same old friend—you were the one who said that first, host.”

The image of the small sphere flickered in the consciousness space, then began to fade.

“Then I’m leaving! Host, wait for my message! Soon! This time it really will be soon!”

“Yes, I believe you.”

Fang Yuan sat on the sofa, the sunlight having moved to the other end of the coffee table.

He looked down at his right hand.

His palm was open.

There was nothing in his palm.

But he knew something was already there.

The pothos on the windowsill swayed gently in the breeze. The water in the glass reflected the dappled sunlight from the ceiling, shining quietly.



Chapter 29 (Bonus): The Bitter Fruit of the Gu Family


After covering up the attack, Fang Yuan stayed home, though this was a pretense; someone with his leisurely nature wouldn't go out unless something urgent came up.

However, after Fang's father learned of Fang Yuan's good relationship with Gu Changming, he urged them to go out. Fang Yuan didn't mind, but Gu Changming seemed to have some things on his plate lately.

He spent his days chatting on the computer or going to the bookstore.

Under the lawyer Fang Yuan hired, the case progressed unexpectedly quickly, concluding almost without any dragging on. Gu Changming also realized for the first time that the foundation left by his family—more precisely, his deceased parents—was far more substantial than he had imagined.

Just as the lawsuit was beginning to take shape, his uncle rushed to his door, his message conveying only one message: settle it privately, absolutely do not take it to court, or his entire family would be ruined.

One day, while Gu Changming was out, his uncle confronted him.

"Changming, I'm begging you, I'm kneeling down."

Seeing that Gu Changming remained unmoved, the middle-aged man grabbed Gu Changming's hand, preparing to kneel. But Gu Chengcai stopped halfway down, his face stiff as he stared at Gu Changming.

"Kneel down, Uncle, why aren't you kneeling?"

Gu Changming looked at the man he had called "Uncle" for almost ten years, watching him freeze in mid-air.

The surrounding pedestrians murmured amongst themselves, watching Gu Changming and Gu Chengcai's performance.

"Are you really not going to show any mercy?"

Gu Chengcai's face twisted as he looked at his nephew, who was completely different from before.

He couldn't understand why things had turned out this way.

After Fang Yuan and Gu Changming visited his house that day, he found out and gave his wife a severe dressing-down.

He scolded her for being so stupid; Gu Changming clearly knew something.

If the kid was still young and inexperienced, she might scold him a bit. But Gu Chengcai, who had worked in an office for so many years and hadn't accomplished anything significant, knew all too well what a teenager might do when he was emotionally agitated.

Otherwise, he wouldn't have brought him things regularly.

Gu Chengcai still felt somewhat guilty towards Gu Changming, but because of his wife's instigation and fear that his nephew might rise to power and take back his house and belongings,

he ignored his family's attitude towards Gu Changming. Occasionally, when he was in a good mood, he would give Gu Changming some money so he could find a place to have fun.

He knew Gu Changming spent his money on internet cafes, but he also…

Later, Liu Hong, a friend of Gu Changming's father, contacted Gu Changming. Since Liu Hong and Gu Cheng had previously visited the Gu family, he knew Liu Hong was Gu Cheng's friend and pretended to be a good uncle in front of him.

This was originally just a way to save face.

Unexpectedly, he seemed quite fond of his deceased brother-in-law, who had helped Gu Changming get into Shi Nan Middle School. Gu Changming, in turn, used this opportunity to get his own son in as well.

Later, when Gu Changming encountered some trouble at work, he also sought his help.

Tsk, Gu Chengcai had to admit that his deceased brother-in-law was quite good at judging people; even after all these years, he still had a good friend.

He had initially intended to treat Gu Changming better out of respect for Liu Hong. However, Liu Hong fell ill after only six months as principal and went to Beijing to recuperate. His wife constantly berated Gu Changming at home, calling him a "jinx" and saying he brought bad luck to those around him. Gu Chengcai had previously dismissed this as mere womanly gossip.

But Liu Hong's illness made him start to have doubts.

Given his brother-in-law's abilities, they shouldn't have ended up dying together. Was his nephew really some kind of jinx?

Later, after Liu Hong left, Gu Chengcai became somewhat jealous, so he turned a blind eye to his wife's behavior.

But unexpectedly, during his two-week business trip, Gu Changming pulled a fast one on him.

He had only been away for two weeks, with only a few days left, when he was summoned back by court. His workplace remained indifferent.

He found out it was someone from his former workplace who had handled that matter.

But wasn't this matter suppressed by Liu Hong?

When he returned, the sky had fallen.

His nephew, accompanied by a lawyer, had come to his door to sue him, claiming something had happened at work.

After thinking it over carefully, he understood.

His nephew had been implicated.

After pleading and begging, nothing worked. It was a colleague he'd worked with for years who finally told him where his nephew was.

Having no other choice, Gu Chengcai had to bite the bullet and come looking for him. He deliberately chose this busy street corner, adopting an extremely humble posture.

After all, blood is thicker than water. Gu Chengcai didn't believe a teenager could be so heartless in front of so many people. Especially with so many eyes watching.

Having worked in the government for so many years, although he hadn't climbed the ranks, dealing with a naive youngster was a piece of cake.

Amidst the whispers of passersby,

"Hey, what's going on?"

"It looks like that uncle is begging that young man."

"What happened?"

Just then, Gu Chengcai suddenly stood up and grabbed Gu Changming's leg, saying,

"Changming, I know, I'm sorry to my brother. I never imagined Ajuan would treat you like that behind your back. Uncle is no human being, no human being at all!

But, we're still family. We're the only ones left in our family."

Hearing this, the passersby began to murmur.

"Sigh, it's pitiful, only the two of them are left in the family."

"That woman is cruel to the child, the uncle might not even know."

"Yes, what family can't overcome their hatred?"

"This child is too heartless, look what he's driven the adults to."

The tide of public opinion quietly turned in favor of Gu Chengcai.

"Yes, we're family."

Gu Changming seemed moved, muttering to himself.

Upon hearing this, Gu Chengcai was secretly delighted. Sure enough, he was only a teenager; his heart was still soft.

At the same time, he thought about Gu Changming's connection to the Huanyu Group, and a rather close one at that.

If he could also latch onto this powerful figure, his future rise to prominence would be just around the corner!

Looking at the pitiful-looking "uncle" before him...

Gu Changming lowered his head, looking at the man he had called "Uncle" for almost ten years. His sensory abilities silently spread out, and the intense, almost overflowing malice and greed emanating from the man surged towards him like a black tide.

What a good uncle he truly is.

"Uncle, you just said you didn't know how Auntie treated me, is that right?"

Gu Changming's voice wasn't loud, but it clearly reached the ears of everyone present.

Did he really not know? As the breadwinner of the family, did he really not know how his wife treated Gu Changming?

Was it possible for someone from his workplace to not know?

Gu Changming had previously believed his uncle didn't know, so when the truth was laid bare before him, he realized he had been deceiving himself.

It was only because in that warehouse-like home, his uncle was the only warmth he could find. He survived by not wanting to trouble his uncle, just having enough to eat.

But now…

“The year before last, during Chinese New Year, my bowl was filled with spoiled leftovers, and you sat across from me eating dumplings, asking me, ‘Why aren’t you eating?’

When I first arrived in your area, my classmates insulted my parents, insulted your sister, and even your nephew and aunt came after them. I forced them to the ground to apologize.”

Gu Changming spoke slowly and deliberately, as if recounting old tragedies unrelated to himself. But with each word, the color drained from Gu Chengcai’s face.

“Tell me—you—don’t know any of this.”

As he spoke, Gu Changming’s pupils widened, his left hand grabbing the middle-aged man’s collar, staring directly into his eyes, speaking each word carefully.

Gu Chengcai was about to throw caution to the wind and shamelessly claim ignorance, but when his nephew picked him up and he saw into his eyes, a fear involuntarily gripped him.

Gu Chengcai was too timid to speak.

The crowd watching this scene began to stir. Those who had overheard their conversation started to whisper.

"This…"

"How could an uncle not know?"

"So he was faking it all just now."

Gu Changming finished speaking, picked up his clothes, and helped him up. He straightened his clothes.

"Uncle doesn't wear this outfit often, does he?"

Gu Chengcai was stunned, not expecting Gu Changming to bring this up.

Gu Changming looked at Gu Chengcai, whose clothes were neat and clean but exuded a cheap feel, and slowly said, "I remember Auntie bought you a Ralph Lauren outfit, didn't she? I remember you liked it a lot, Uncle. You always wore those two-piece outfits when we had guests or friends, didn't you? Why aren't you wearing it today? Is it because you think I'm not worthy?"

"Or do you think it's not suitable for today?"

Gu Chengcai's face turned somewhat ugly after saying that. Gu Changming was right; he did like that Ralph Lauren outfit, but it wasn't appropriate for today. This outfit was a cheap 20-yuan bargain from a roadside stall, meant to make him look like his nephew, to show his humility to others.

"Uncle, weren't you going to kneel?"

Gu Changming looked down at him, his gaze as calm as a bottomless pool, watching another clumsy clown's performance.

"Why aren't you kneeling anymore? Is there too few people? Don't you want to kneel?"

Gu Chengcai's facial muscles twitched violently a few times, his fist clenched, then relaxed.

He knelt. Kneeled before his nephew, a high school sophomore kneeling before him in front of everyone.

If Gu Changming had relented, Gu Chengcai wouldn't have been so reluctant, but he could feel the way the people around him were looking at him like he was a clown.

"I..."

He slowly raised his head to look at the boy opposite him, the feigned sorrow on his face completely gone, replaced by a gloomy, almost ferocious expression. He looked at the boy before him as if he were truly seeing him for the first time.

"Fine, very well," Gu Chengcai gritted his teeth, the voice squeezed out from between them, "You've grown up, do you really have to be this ruthless?"

Gu Changming didn't reply, just looked at him calmly.

In his perception, the malice emanating from the other was no longer concealed, like a snake cornered against a wall, hissing and flicking its tongue.

But he was no longer a helpless toddler. The croaking of a defeated dog, a barely audible bark, echoed.

Gu Chengcai suddenly sneered, lowering his voice, "You think everything's fine just because you've latched onto Huanyu Group? Let me tell you, that water runs deep. A mere brat like you might drown without even knowing it."

"No need for Uncle's concern," Gu Changming brushed non-existent dust off his trousers, as if brushing away something that had gotten on him when he was hugged earlier. "Uncle should worry about himself. The court summons won't wait for anyone."

With that, he turned and left.

Behind him came Gu Chengcai's suppressed, almost distorted voice: "Gu Changming! Don't you have any lingering affection?"

Gu Changming paused.

He didn't turn around, only turned his face to the side, his voice carried back by the wind, clear and calm:

"Let you go?"

"Uncle, back then—who let me go?"

The crowd automatically parted to make way. The boy's thin figure gradually walked away, blending into the light and shadow at the end of the street.

Gu Cheng stood alone, his face ashen. The looks from the passersby had changed; the whispers and pointing were no longer hushed, but felt like needles pricking him.

In the restaurant across the street, Fang Yuan watched this scene and nodded with satisfaction.

"You've grown up."

Attorney Hu, standing nearby, tried hard to maintain his composure, but inwardly thought:

Isn't the young master about the same age as this Gu student?

He'd only ever heard of "daddy's boyfriends," was this a "daddy's friend"?

Attorney Hu dismissed these jumbled thoughts, cleared his throat, and said,

"Young Master, it seems we're no longer needed. Young Master Gu handled it himself."

Fang Yuan, reflecting on Gu Changming's growth, thought, "No wonder the male lead matures so quickly."

He should be able to handle things independently soon, but until then, as his senior, he should help him keep things in order.

"Handled it? The court summons hasn't arrived yet."

There's no reason why Gu Chengcai hasn't been promoted after all these years. It's one thing he lived off his nephew's ill-gotten gains, at least he was fed, but everyone in his workplace knows about his family's messy affairs. If Liu Hong hadn't left quickly, his scandals would have been exposed long ago.

But his superiors know. It's one thing that Gu Chengcai is mediocre, but someone who helped his family with debts and entrusted their child to him. His house and many expenses were contributed by this person, and this is how he treats their child?

He's morally bankrupt, mediocre, and comes from a terrible family.

Anyone with a brain wouldn't promote someone like him. He's only staying in that company because Liu Hong helped them settle a matter, and their superiors turned a blind eye, treating him like he was freeloading.

Now things have come to light.

Heh, his family troubles have brought him a lot of trouble, and it's not like there aren't people in his workplace who dislike him. Even if there aren't, it's unlikely anyone will offer help when he's down, but there's no shortage of people who will kick him when he's down.

And I heard he recently received a sum of money. A small business offended someone, and I heard their leader had connections, so they gave the whole company a sum of money, except for Gu Chengcai and a few others.

This kind of thing wouldn't normally be a big deal; he wouldn't be able to do much with the money, at most he'd just be a messenger.

But now…

Attorney Hu immediately understood after hearing Fang Yuan's words.

“It’s all organized,” Attorney Hu said, “Time, place, amount, person involved. Every detail has a source. Also—” He paused, “His leader’s side is also fine.”

This matter, even without the Huanyu Group's involvement, could have been resolved in the time it takes for Liu Hong to make a phone call.

Fang Yuan nodded.

⋛(▀Ĺ̯ ▀-͠ )~⋚

Attorney Hu: ദ്ദി˶ｰ̀֊ｰ́ )✧

After indicating receipt, he picked up his briefcase and went straight to Gu Chengcai. Standing before Gu Chengcai, he said loudly,

"Excuse me, are you Mr. Gu Chengcai?"

Gu Chengcai, who had been in a bad mood and wanted to curse, softened his tone upon seeing Attorney Hu's well-dressed suit and gleaming shoes.

"This is me. What can I do for you?"

Attorney Hu delivered a message that left Gu Chengcai in despair.

"Hello, I've been invited to investigate your bribery case."

"What!"

He then explained the situation to him.

After hearing this, Gu Chengcai's expression froze.

Gu Chengcai suddenly understood something.

From beginning to end, he thought he was fighting his nephew—a naive teenager, someone he thought he could easily manipulate.

But the person standing before him was never Gu Changming.

In the end, he had to swallow the bitter fruit of his own actions.



Chapter 30 (Bonus): The Fang Family's Plans


With Gu Changming's matter settled, let's see what the Fang family is up to.

A deafening sound erupted from the Fang family home early in the morning.

"What!"

Fang Xiuxiu stared in shock at Fang Chenxu and his wife, who were rarely home, and stammered,

"Dad, say it again."

Fang Chenxu and his wife exchanged a glance. Fang Chenxu sighed and said, "You and Yuanyuan aren't siblings."

This time, Fang Xiuxiu heard it clearly and looked at her mother in disbelief. Zhang Xia nodded helplessly.

"It's true."

Confirming her parents' stance, Fang Xiuxiu slumped into a mahogany chair, her eyes unfocused. After a long while, she murmured, "Oh my god, I was right..."

I really am not Dad's biological child.

I knew Dad and Fang Yuan were so great; all he has is good looks.

No, I'm not even as good-looking as Fang Yuan (┳Д┳)

Seeing Fang Xiuxiu like this, Zhang Xia felt heartbroken. She went over and hugged Fang Xiuxiu, comforting her, "It's okay, it's okay, you're all Mommy's children."

While comforting her, she glared at Fang Chenxu. It was all this guy's fault; why did he have to say it out loud? It's just another illegitimate child, right? If she had just explained it to him, she wouldn't have cared. It's all fake anyway.

Seeing Zhang Xia's look, Fang Chenxu silently lowered his head. He couldn't help it; both mother and daughter were suffering, so he had to blame him.

After news of Gu Changming's situation reached him, information about him appeared on his desk. He collected DNA samples from Fang Yuan and Gu Changming for testing.

The results showed they were related.

Well, he hadn't been wrong.

The good news was that even though their biological parents were probably gone, his son Fang Yuan was still his son.

The bad news was that he had a brother.

In fact, Fang Chenxu and his wife had prepared themselves mentally before hearing the news, given Fang Yuan's friendly attitude towards Gu Changming and their similar appearances.

They were prepared for this result. Knowing how Gu Changming was treated in the Gu family, Fang Chenxu and his wife were relieved that Fang Yuan hadn't ended up in the Gu family. Otherwise, with Gu Changming's treatment, how could their Yuan Yuan, whom they doted on like a precious gem, possibly bear the same fate as Gu Changming!

The thought of Fang Yuan living like Gu Changming made Zhang Xia, and even Fang Chenxu, want to have the Gu family buried alive.

Fang Chenxu and his wife felt that since their parents were both dead and their other child was already living such a life, adopting Fang Yuan was actually a good deed.

Then they faced a dilemma: what to do with Gu Changming?

If they didn't know each other well, Fang Chenxu considered giving him some money to get rid of him. He didn't want it to affect their Yuanyuan. As for letting the Gu family take advantage of the situation, well, given how they treated Gu Changming, they couldn't even imagine what Fang Yuan's life would be like if he went to live with them.

When Zhang Xia found out, she took Fang Yuan to Gu Changming's house and wanted nothing more than to throw them both into the sea.

Right now, the two brothers probably didn't know the situation, but since they were close, they couldn't do anything.

After much thought, they decided to be honest with Fang Xiuxiu, otherwise, she might discover the problem and expose them someday.

Knowing their daughter's temperament, if she discovers the truth, it's fine, but if she only knows a little bit, who knows what kind of trouble she might cause.

"Waaah, Mom."

"My good child."

Zhang Xia hugged Fang Xiuxiu, her heart aching. These two children had grown up together for so many years, and suddenly learning that the other wasn't right was hard to accept.

But a short, sharp pain was better than a long, drawn-out one. It was better to tell her now, otherwise, the truth would eventually come out and cause a huge mess.

Fang Xiuxiu timidly asked,

"Waaah, can I still call you Mom?"

Zhang Xia's face, which was originally kind, turned angry upon hearing this. She pinched her ear.

"You brat, what are you saying? I'm your mother! I wasted ten months of my life carrying you!"

"Ouch, ouch, ouch!"

Fang Xiuxiu pretended to be in pain, but in fact, Zhang Xia hadn't used any force at all.

She suddenly realized,

"Oh, how come I'm the eldest?"

The eldest?

Upon hearing those two words, Zhang Xia stopped pinching her ear and gave Fang Xiuxiu a solid slap.

"You brat, where did you learn that word? It sounds more feudal than my own mother!"

"Hehe." Fang Xiuxiu covered the spot where she had been slapped, her eyes darting around as she began to plot.

"You little rascal, you've given your sister something to use against you!"

"No wonder he thought Fang Yuan was different from me. I thought it was because I wasn't good enough, but it turns out it's because he's too good."

"Haha, little brother, this is perfect for your older sister to squeeze a little dry..."

Fang Xiuxiu hadn't had time to indulge in her fantasies for long before her strict father's iron fist struck her down.

"Bang!"

"Ah! Dad, what are you doing! Are you trying to murder your own daughter?"

Fang Xiuxiu covered her head and dodged to the side, glaring fiercely at Fang Chenxu.

Fang Chenxu couldn't help but cover his face. He didn't know who his daughter took after; she was full of clever and mischievous ideas. Just looking at her expression, this father knew without a second thought what kind of trouble she was planning.

"What a misfortune for the family! What a misfortune for the family!"

Hearing Fang Chenxu's words, Fang Xiuxiu retorted, "Who wants to inherit your company? Other young ladies are all doing art, design, and fine arts. What young lady goes to work on a construction site carrying bricks!

That kid Fang Yuan, he's learning piano, art, and attending training centers—he's seen way more and better than me! I want to be an artistic young man too!"

Fang Chenxu glared at Fang Xiuxiu, somewhat amused and exasperated. In other families, people fight for power and inheritance, but in his family, none of them seem interested in such things. Was his family harmonious, or was it simply unfortunate?

Zhang Xia, standing to the side, also spoke up, shattering her illusions.

"Girl, wake up. With your talent, others can draw an egg, while you can't even draw a proper circle. And the piano, Yuan Yuan could play in less than two hours, but you..."

She pressured Yuan Yuan's teacher, Zhang Xia, to either teach only one person or change teachers.

There was no way around it; one could play it after just one look and one try, while the other couldn't even recognize all 88 keys—the difference was too great.

Zhang Xia, trying to save face for Fang Xiuxiu, didn't finish her sentence, but Fang Xiuxiu knew what her mother wanted to say. Her face flushed red, and she blurted out things like, "That guy is inhuman!" "Art requires a lot of practice!" "I was only a few years old when I learned to paint; that was just an extreme case," and other incomprehensible remarks.

Zhang Xia, listening nearby, couldn't help but laugh.

Fang Chenxu, on the other hand, couldn't help but laugh. He remembered when Fang Xiuxiu had been clamoring to learn piano, and they thought they'd name her Fang Yuan, not favoring one child over the other.

But the teacher had a long face and said either one of them should be taught, or they'd have to switch teachers.

He thought the teacher was favoring one, but after sitting in on one class, he realized he couldn't blame the teacher.

While Fang Xiuxiu was still struggling with her left and right hands, Fang Yuan had already started playing etudes; the same thing happened when they painted.

To be honest, Fang Xiuxiu had only normal talent, but unfortunately, her comparison was a monster—someone who picked things up so quickly, as if she'd never played before.

Compared to her father, Fang Xiuxiu was utterly outmatched.

When people are emotionally agitated, their senses are heightened. Hearing her father's laughter, Fang Xiuxiu wanted to disappear into thin air.

She threw a tantrum, rolling on the ground:

"I don't care! I don't care! What kind of daughter works on a construction site while her son plays the piano and paints? Is that right?! This is discrimination! And who said I don't have artistic talent? I dance very well, don't I? My teacher often praises me!"

"Yes, yes, yes, my darling, my beautiful darling."

Dance is half about looks, and half about figure. Fang Xiuxiu, without a doubt, inherited her parents' good genes and is now a graceful young woman. Her basic dance training already puts her ahead of half the other test-takers.

Besides, didn't you train at our family's dance school? Silly girl, of course she'd praise you…

The Fang family has a son and a daughter; people say they are a perfect family, talented in both academics and sports, a handsome couple.

At first glance, it seems like a compliment to her children's success, but those who know a little about the family know that "both scholarly and athletic, a handsome man and a beautiful woman" actually refers mostly to her youngest son.

"Both scholarly and athletic, a handsome man and a beautiful woman"—one person embodies seven of these qualities.

Fang Xiuxiu only embodies the "woman" part; she doesn't even qualify as "beautiful." Oh well, what can you do? Her Yuanyuan is just too good-looking.

When Zhang Xia started her training program, Fang Yuan had just gained some recognition, so she promoted it extensively.

Wow, the effect was amazing! Everyone was asking for her son's contact information, whether he was famous yet, and what kind of woman he liked.

Nobody cared about awards or anything like that, so the couple quickly removed Fang Yuan's pictures to avoid being targeted.

He just turned 18 this year, and a whole bunch of people are already contacting him, practically wearing down his doorstep.

Sigh, sometimes having such an outstanding child has its downsides.

(｡＞∀＜｡)

Fang Xiuxiu recovered from the shock, suddenly straightened her expression, and sincerely promised, "Dad, don't worry, I will definitely treat Fang Yuan well from now on."

Fang Chenxu looked at the "sincere" expression on his daughter's face and slapped his forehead—he knew his daughter too well; no matter how sweet her words were, the mischievous intent on her face was practically overflowing.

This silly girl is probably plotting something again. He immediately put on a stern face, sternly stopping her from uttering her thoughts, and then told her the whole story about Gu Changming and Fang Yuan.

This time, it was Fang Xiuxiu's turn to get really nervous.

Could her brother have run off with someone else?

She grabbed Fang Chenxu's sleeve anxiously: "Dad, how about we take some money and send the Gu family abroad? If that doesn't work, like in the movies, we can find some people to..."

Before she could finish, Fang Chenxu glared at her fiercely.

"Put away those crazy thoughts and calm down."

"If he doesn't get better, how will I mooch off him!"

Fang Chenxu was somewhat relieved by the first part; Fang Xiuxiu, as his older sister, still cared about her brother. But what did his silly daughter mean by that last sentence?

"Sigh, alright, alright, Dad has taken care of this for you. Just keep that to yourself."

Fang Xiuxiu made a zipping motion, indicating she understood.

After Zhang Xia dismissed Fang Xiuxiu, only Fang Chenxu and his wife remained in the living room. Zhang Xia sat down beside him and asked in a low voice, "What are you planning to do about the Gu family?"

Fang Chenxu leaned back on the sofa, tapping his fingers on the armrest, his tone as calm as if he were discussing a perfectly ordinary business deal.

“They're expanding into Southeast Asia and need a few on-site staff. Aren't the Gu family always trying to get ahead? Just give them project manager titles and send them over.”

Zhang Xia nodded, not commenting on their willingness.

With their family's group's size, they were local bigwigs in the city. They were in the civil engineering business, with plenty of capable men under their command.

Millions of workers were their livelihood.

If it weren't for his family, the Gu family wouldn't even have the right to meet Fang Chenxu, let alone be mentioned.

Zhang Xia was silent for a moment, then sighed softly. She knew her husband was never a saint. If it weren't for Fang Yuan, how could someone who made his fortune in real estate be so “merciful” to a complete stranger's family? Calling them project managers was basically sending them to the frontier.

Once they were there, far from the reach of the authorities, it would be difficult for them to cause any trouble.

"The salary, based on local standards, is enough to support a family of three, and the company covers the child's education expenses. Do you think the Gu couple, given their current situation, would refuse?"

With the court summons and the employment issue, Gu Chengcai is almost homeless in the area and is already planning to move. Now that Fang Chenxu has spoken, someone will naturally take care of it.

"What about Gu Changming? Have you asked his opinion?"

"We'll see after the court's ruling." Fang Chenxu put down his teacup. "But I think he'll agree."

He spoke with an air of certainty. He knew Gu Changming inside and out—after years of enduring humiliation in the Gu family, the fact that he could befriend Fang Yuan meant he wasn't just anyone.

Now that he was offering him a gift, along with a free ticket to escape, there was no reason for the kid to refuse.

As for that couple, did they want to save money to come back? Did they want to turn their lives around? Did they want to harass his Yuan Yuan again?

Although the chances were slim, Fang Chenxu, in charge of the group, wouldn't let any opportunity slip by.

Especially since it concerns his family, he hoped they would be sensible, otherwise…

Fang Chenxu twirled the ring on his finger, his eyes indifferent.

…

That evening at dinner, the family of four sat around the table, the atmosphere as harmonious as ever. Fang Chenxu picked up a piece of food with his chopsticks and casually suggested, “Yuanyuan, why don’t you take advantage of the holiday and go out for a trip with your friend Gu Changming?”

Fang Yuan responded with a nod, not giving it much thought.

Fang Xiuxiu kept her head down, shoveling rice into her mouth, trying hard to suppress the surging gossip urge within her. Her gaze darted back and forth between her father and younger brother, watching their nonchalant performance. Only one thought crossed her mind—goodness, her father's acting skills were such a waste; he was a real talent for acting if he wasn't an Oscar winner.

At the same time, she carefully observed Fang Yuan, and had to admit, her younger brother was quite handsome.

She then thought of herself. Sigh.

Fang Yuan and Fang Chenxu chatted idly, eventually bringing up the Gu family. Fang Chenxu felt it was about time and didn't want to play any games with his family, so he directly stated his plans.

Fang Yuan didn't have any particular ideas, only saying he would discuss it with Gu Changming.

Then the family discussed the matter.

Fang Chenxu looked at Fang Xiuxiu, who was still eating, and said, "Eat slowly, no one's going to take it from you."

Fang Xiuxiu remained silent, just continuing to eat, afraid she wouldn't be able to control herself. She hadn't expected her father to be so decisive; he had just said yesterday that he would bring her younger brother over for dinner tonight.

"Isn't the point of dance to maintain a good figure?"

"Ahem."



Chapter 31 The Stepping Stone for the Male Protagonist in a Wuxia Novel: The Holy Son (Beginning)


Fang Yuan suddenly opened his eyes, feeling an unbearable ache all over his body, as if he had been run over by a carriage. He struggled to sit up, but found his body incredibly weak; even the slightest movement aggravated his wounds, causing him to grimace in pain.

Fang Yuan looked around and found himself in a dense forest, surrounded by tall trees and thick grass. Sunlight filtered through the leaves, creating dappled patterns of light.

Memories flooded back.

Time rewound to after resolving Gu Changming's matter. Fang Yuan had spent some time with his parents and even visited his maternal grandparents, Zhang Jianguo and Zhang Jianguo, spending time with them.

As for Gu Changming, after dealing with that vampire family, he was refreshed and invigorated. In his words,

"I lack nothing now."

Therefore, after witnessing Gu Changming's actions firsthand, Fang Yuan felt immense satisfaction towards him.

I heard he's been really into a girl in his class lately, and they're talking about going for a walk in the mountains.

After settling some things, System 120 arrived.

"Ta-da, Host, I'm back."

System 120 returned one afternoon.

It then explained their mission to Fang Yuan.

"Host, this mission was something I managed to get from my teacher after a lot of effort."

Golden ripples appeared on the surface of the small white orb.

The orb then explained the mission to Fang Yuan.

The mission was to travel to a martial arts world, become the stepping stone and holy son of the male protagonist, witnessing his growth. It would take a relatively long time.

It also explained that missions in this world take a long time, so the orb had been piling up for a while. He asked his teacher, System 100, to help him choose one.

Although other mission takers would consider this mission incredibly long and tedious, his teacher, System 100, said it was the most suitable mission for their current situation.

"You're currently sitting on a treasure trove, but without the tools or specific knowledge. This task is a good option for you."

Hearing System 120's explanation, Fang Yuan nodded thoughtfully.

Indeed, as System 120 had stated, they should now use the tools to excavate the legacy within him.

Currently, the two of them lacked understanding of a complete extraordinary system and a proper sense of what a normal task should be.

This task met their requirements: it was time-consuming, had a complete system, and perfectly suited their needs.

Seeing Fang Yuan nod, System 120 said, "Then let's not delay, we need to set off immediately."

"So soon?"

A helpless expression appeared on System 120's pristine white surface (｡-人-｡).

"There's no way around it, the host's space is incredibly busy. If this mission weren't so long and tedious, we wouldn't have gotten a good one."

It quickly added, "Host, don't worry about your family. Although we're only beginners, my influence as the world's will can still minimize your presence for now, so your family won't worry about you."

Hearing this, Fang Yuan felt relieved. He drafted a message about going on a trip and sent it to his family and friends.

System 120, wanting to allay Fang Yuan's concerns, continued, "And this time there won't be any body reconstruction. This time we're using soul transmigration, so even if we fail, there won't be any consequences."

System 120 and Fang Yuan were no longer the same as before. Although their physical size wasn't as large, their rank was genuinely high.

The loss from a single failed mission was negligible, and they didn't need to worry about the failure harming the mission world.

What significant impact could a mere extra, a background character, have on the protagonist and the world? Don't be ridiculous, this isn't something an extra could do.

Hearing System 120 say this, Fang Yuan had nothing to say.

"Alright, let's prepare to set off then."

System 120's platinum surface began to fluctuate, the proportion of gold increasing.

The colleague added,

“This time, you won't be fighting alone, Host. Although I can't be by your side every moment during this mission, I will still wholeheartedly assist you.”

“It's okay, I… What? That's not what the manual says, is it?”

“Ah, didn't I tell you? Oh no! The passage has opened, Host, we have to go first. Otherwise, it will affect…”

Hearing this, Fang Yuan, unable to provide full assistance, realized what was happening and interrupted, “Wait, I still want to…”

After a moment of dizziness, Fang Yuan found himself in this deep forest.

Recovering, in Fang Yuan's consciousness space,

Fang Yuan was frantically shaking System 120's body.

“When did you tell me this?”

System 120 said with a hint of grievance,

“I updated the contents of the manual before I left.”

Hearing this, Fang Yuan weakly released System 120.

"You didn't tell me. Never mind, let's think about what to do now."

System 120, feeling somewhat apologetic, said, "I'm sorry, host, it was me..."

"It's not your fault, I didn't notice the changes in the manual."

Fang Yuan composed himself. Complaining was pointless now; what he should do was figure out how to change the situation, not complain.

"Host~, you're so kind."

System 120 looked at Fang Yuan with teary eyes, secretly resolving to assist him properly.

Fang Yuan, supporting his half-crippled body, surveyed his surroundings.

Fang Yuan was currently in a deep forest, his body covered in wounds of varying sizes, his clothes tattered.

"120, what's the situation?"

The system 120's childish, somewhat timid voice echoed in his mind:

"Host, we have good news and bad news. Which do you want to hear?"

Fang Yuan glanced at his scars and physical condition. "Let's hear the bad news first. It can't get much worse now."

Fang Yuan sensed that his physical condition was quite poor, the kind where he could only hold on for a little longer.

Upon hearing this, System 120 said, "The bad news is, whether it's because this mission has been delayed for too long or because the passage is unstable, we've strayed from our original timeline and arrived forty years before the story began."

"But, the good news is..."

"Does that mean our activity time is longer?"

Before System 120 could finish speaking, Fang Yuan said speechlessly.

"That's correct, but..."

"But I'll pretend I'm going to be there in the next second."

Fang Yuan forced himself to stay conscious, using this conversation to maintain his last vestiges of clarity.

"No, host, that's part of it, but what I want to say is that when my channel node shifted, I selected an exceptionally superior object for you! And because the protagonist hasn't appeared yet, our position's influence on this world is still there, so it can..."

Fang Yuan listened to System 120's words, but his consciousness became increasingly blurred towards the end.

An exceptionally superior object?

Fang Yuan thought it was an exceptionally tragic object; he felt he was about to...not...hold...to...go...off...bye...too.

Before System 120 could finish speaking, Fang Yuan lost consciousness and collapsed to the ground with a thud.

In his fading consciousness, only one thought raced through Fang Yuan's mind:

Looks like his venture has started off badly; he's dying before he's even halfway through, no… it should be, he's dying the moment he steps out the door.

“Host, hold on! People are coming soon!”

Seeing Fang Yuan collapse, System 120 frantically jumped up and down in the spatial dimension.

In the distance, deep in the dense forest, several figures seemed to be rushing towards them.

“Quick, quick, there are children escaping that way. Chasing after them might still save them.”

At this moment, System 120 was pacing anxiously in the consciousness space. The partners it had chosen for Fang Yuan were hastily selected, but in its opinion, weren't they extremely outstanding?

Now it seems they're about to be eliminated Σ(ŎдŎ|||)ﾉﾉ

"No, we can't go any further."

System 120 gritted its teeth and stamped its foot. Ripples spread across its golden surface as a small golden ball of energy was extracted from its body.

"Host, don't worry... I won't—let you collapse here!"

System 120 sensed Fang Yuan's consciousness fading and realized that placing its hopes on the reinforcements was unwise.

For Fang Yuan's sake, System 120 decided to send it to save him, extracting a wisp of world essence and letting it float into Fang Yuan's body.

"Waaah, my money."

Feeling Fang Yuan's condition gradually improving, System 120 felt a pang of regret but still thought it was worth it.

At least, it had saved its host...

"Senior brother, there's a child here!"

A young man dressed in black exclaimed upon seeing Fang Yuan.

Upon hearing the voice, a young man dressed in simple clothes with his hair tied in a square bun hurriedly asked,

"Where?"

The young man's eyes were sharp; he immediately spotted Fang Yuan lying among the clan members.

The young man led the way, and the two reached Fang Yuan. The young man carefully picked Fang Yuan up and tested his condition with his inner energy.

"Senior brother, how is he..."

"There's still hope. Although his breath is weak, but..."

Mu Chen's words trailed off. Seeing this, the young man Xiao Tian assumed Fang Yuan hadn't made it, and gritted his teeth: "Sigh, he didn't make it... those damned bandits!"

The young man didn't reply, because he sensed from Fang Yuan that his life force was gradually rising, albeit very slowly, but Mu Chen had definitely felt it.

It was extremely faint, yet undeniably present. If it weren't for the fact that their Hunyuan Sect valued martial arts, and Mu Chen's exceptional talent and astonishing perception, he wouldn't have been able to detect it; others wouldn't have noticed.

"The child is alright," Mu Chen suppressed his doubts and said in a deep voice, "Let's go meet Master first."

Xiao Tian breathed a sigh of relief upon hearing this.

The two carefully picked up Fang Yuan and sped towards the edge of the dense forest. Soon, they met up with a slender, refined-looking middle-aged man. This man was none other than the Grand Elder of the Hunyuan Sect, Mu Chen and Xiao Tian's master—Mu Jingxing.

"Master, we found a child who escaped from bandits," Mu Chen gently set Fang Yuan down and briefly explained the situation in a low voice.

Mu Jingxing stepped forward, his gaze sweeping over Fang Yuan's wounded body, his brows furrowing slightly. He placed his hand on Fang Yuan's pulse, and after a moment, the wrinkles between his brows deepened.
