His right palm rose like a knife, aimed straight for Fang Yuan's throat—the Thousand Gold Slash, taking the shortest and most ruthless route.

Xue Shaoyan of Qingyun Medical Clinic took a different path. He didn't attack head-on, but instead cut in from the flank, his ten fingers bent like hooks, the fingertips carrying a faint layer of blue energy.

That was Qingyun Medical Clinic's "Pulse-Severing Hand," specifically targeting the body's meridian points. Once seized, the meridians would be paralyzed, leaving the victim completely helpless.

Liu Chuanping of the Shennong Sect pressed forward from the other side. His martial arts style leaned towards fierce power; his fists, like hammers, created a whistling sound as he delivered a powerful, heavy blow aimed directly at Fang Yuan's ribs.

Su Wantang of the Hundred Flowers Valley attacked from behind. Her martial arts possessed the unique lightness and elegance of the Hundred Flowers Valley, unleashing a flurry of palm strikes, a mix of feints and real attacks, making it impossible to distinguish which was the real strike.

Disciples from other sects also displayed their skills—some channeled their inner energy into their fists, some used grappling techniques to lock joints, some attacked from the ground down, and some even picked up low stools used for resting on the sidelines and slammed them down on Fang Yuan's head.

The attacks from fifteen people landed simultaneously from all directions, leaving almost no blind spots.

Fang Yuan stood at the center of the storm.

He did not choose to dodge; instead, he took a step forward.

The internal energy of the Hunyuan Gong surged through his meridians like a tidal wave, his muscles and fascia tensing and relaxing simultaneously in that instant, forming a profoundly mysterious state of energy accumulation.

It was stretched to its limit in that instant—he could hear the nine illusions and one reality in Su Wantang's palm strike behind him, feel the trajectory of Xue Shaoyan's finger strike from the side, and catch the vortex of air created by Ji Mingzhao's palm strike from the front.

Then he moved.

The Tendon-Dislocating Bone Hand.

Not a point-to-point counterattack, but a continuous, fluid movement.

His left hand reached out from an impossible angle, his five fingers gripping the wrist of a disciple charging at him, and with a flick and pull—the disciple felt as if his wrist was bound by an iron chain, his entire body involuntarily thrown out, knocking over two people beside him.

At the same time, Fang Yuan lightly tapped the ground with his right foot, using the momentum to spin half a circle. His right elbow thrust out like a spear, slamming into another disciple's chest.

It wasn't a forceful strike, but the penetrating power went straight to his spine. The disciple groaned, staggering back seven or eight steps before landing hard on his backside.

Ji Mingzhao's Thousand Gold Strike had arrived.

Fang Yuan didn't dodge. He raised his hand, catching the blow with the back of his palm.

Not blocking, but receiving.

Ji Mingzhao felt as if his palm had sliced ​​into a piece of thoroughly soaked, tanned leather. All the force was dissolved and dissolved layer by layer, leaving only a tingling sensation traveling from his palm back to his wrist.

How could this be?!

He didn't have time to figure it out, because Fang Yuan's counterattack had already arrived.

Fang Yuan's hand flipped over smoothly, his five fingers gripping Ji Mingzhao's wrist like iron pincers. Ji Mingzhao was shocked, taking three quick steps to barely dodge, but his wrist was still grazed by the fingertips, leaving a red mark that stung painfully.

Xue Shaoyan's Severing Pulse Hand lashed out from the side, his ten fingers radiating a vibrant blue aura. Fang Yuan didn't even turn around; he subtly pulled his left shoulder back three inches, allowing the fingers to miss, then slammed his shoulder back—the sinking force of the Hunyuan Gong flowed from his shoulder into Xue Shaoyan's palm. Xue Shaoyan felt as if he had struck an iron wall, his tiger's mouth trembling violently.

Liu Chuanping's Mountain-Moving Hammer arrived, its heavy force striking Fang Yuan's ribs. Fang Yuan pressed down with his right hand, palm and fist colliding with a dull thud, like someone striking a stone slab with a cloth-wrapped hammer.

Liu Chuanping felt as if his punch had struck a mountain, the force sinking deep into the earth, while Fang Yuan remained completely unmoved.

Su Wantang's palm shadows were still swirling in the air. Fang Yuan didn't bother to discern the feints, but instead took a step forward—a step extremely cunning, landing precisely on the point where her palm strikes shifted, instantly dissipating most of the palm shadows.

Su Wantang's expression changed slightly, and she hurriedly withdrew her palms and retreated, but Fang Yuan didn't pursue her, instead continuing to move towards his next target.

Fang Yuan moved like a fish, weaving through the encirclement of fifteen people.

Although Fang Yuan, having comprehended the essence of life, didn't cultivate a technique particularly suited for offense, his endurance and recovery were unparalleled.

Especially after comprehending that particular state of mind, his stamina and recovery had reached a new level.

Each step landed on a gap in the encirclement formation, each attack disrupting someone's rhythm, and those who were opened up tripped up those behind them.

The fifteen people were like meticulously arranged chess pieces, and Fang Yuan was dismantling them one by one.

These sect elites all fell into Fang Yuan's rhythm.

One disciple was knocked back by Fang Yuan's sudden burst of energy, colliding with another disciple behind him, both losing their balance simultaneously. On the other side, a disciple's sweeping kick missed, striking his own comrade's thigh instead, causing both to fall to the ground.

The three charging from the front were tangled together, their punches and kicks interfering with each other. Fang Yuan didn't even need to lift a finger; he simply sidestepped to clear the way, and they collided into a chaotic heap.

The scene transformed from fifteen against one into a chaotic chase. Fewer and fewer could keep up with Fang Yuan's pace, more and more were tripped up by their own men, and more and more lost their footing.

The time it takes to brew a cup of tea passed.

Only five people remained standing.

After a moment, only three remained.

Fang Yuan withdrew his palm strike from a disciple's shoulder. The man staggered backward, his legs giving way, and he knelt on one knee. He gasped for breath and looked up—only he and two others remained.

Ji Mingzhao stood to the left front, sweat beading on his forehead, but his breathing remained steady. The unique breathing technique of the Thousand Gold Pavilion had allowed him to conserve his strength during the earlier melee. His clothes were dusty, but his eyes remained clear.

Su Wantang stood to the right front, her long hair slightly disheveled, a few strands falling across her forehead. Her hands remained in a defensive stance. Her breathing was more rapid than Ji Mingzhao's, but her eyes showed no panic, only a focused vigilance.

Fang Yuan looked at the two of them, and for the first time, he stopped. From the start until now, his breathing had remained steady, not a single bead of sweat on his forehead.

"Not bad," he said.

This was the first thing he had said since the start of the event.

Ji Mingzhao didn't answer, but slowly adjusted his breathing, raising his right palm again. Su Wantang gently exhaled a breath of stale air, her toes slightly apart, her center of gravity lowered.

The two of them, one on the left and one on the right, flanked the boy in the center.

The audience stands on the sidelines were deathly silent. No one spoke, no one discussed, even their breathing was suppressed to a minimum. Everyone held their breath, waiting for the final moment to arrive.

The morning breeze in the martial arts arena grew stronger, causing the surrounding flags to flutter. The sun had risen higher, shining down from directly above, compressing the shadows of the three people in the arena into three small round spots.

Fang Yuan stood there, his back to the sun, his features hidden in shadow. He looked at Ji Mingzhao and Su Wantang, a slight twitch at the corner of his mouth.

Then he raised a hand and beckoned to them.

“Come.”

Ji Mingzhao’s eyes narrowed, and he sprinted forward with a powerful step, his figure shooting out like an arrow. Su Wantang moved simultaneously, gracefully appearing from the other side, her palms striking out in unison, the Hundred Flowers Palm Shadow blooming in the air once more.

Their combined attack was one forceful, one gentle; one orthodox, one unpredictable.

Fang Yuan took a deep breath, sensing the flow of energy around him.

In the stands, everyone held their breath.



Chapter 48 The Stepping Stone for the Wuxia Male Protagonist: The Holy Son 18


Fang Yuan stood rooted to the spot, sensing the attacks from both men.

Su Wantang and Ji Mingzhao were both exceptional talents. Fang Yuan could sense that their inner energy was nearing the third realm, only lacking the comprehension of intent; their qi channels were practically within reach.

Based on previous years' standards, these two were considered favorites to win the championship.

Their inner energy surged ceaselessly through their meridians, like a mountain stream overflowing with water, its calm surface concealing overwhelming power.

Ji Mingzhao's attack was already close at hand.

During the exchange, Ji Mingzhao deeply felt the pressure emanating from Fang Yuan.

He was unbelievably strong.

Among his peers, Ji Mingzhao would call him the strongest. He retracted his earlier accusation that Fang Yuan was arrogant; Fang Yuan had the right to say so.

If it were a one-on-one fight, Ji Mingzhao would have obediently conceded defeat within a few rounds against Fang Yuan.

But…

Qian Jin Bu took seven consecutive steps, each leaving a shallow footprint on the Qinggang rock. His figure blurred into five afterimages as he charged, his right palm raised like a blade, his left hidden beneath his ribs—this was the true killing move of the Qian Jin Pavilion, the "Double Slash Combo." The first slash was a feint, the second a real strike, a feint within a real strike, a real strike within a feint. No more than three of his generation could truly discern this combo.

He, Ji Mingzhao, was the number one talent of the Qian Jin Pavilion in his generation. Whether in pharmacology or martial arts, he was number one.

Admired by his peers, cherished by his teachers, and anticipated by his sect, his life had been smooth sailing until the Medicine King Valley Tournament began.

But then he encountered Fang Yuan, a prodigy whose pharmacology and martial arts skills were undeniably superior to his own.

Ji Mingzhao knew very well that with Fang Yuan's talent and his age, he was now the closest he could get to Fang Yuan.

He had to consider whether this was his only chance to defeat Fang Yuan in his lifetime.

So…

“Get down!”

At the same time, Su Wantang attacked from the right.

The Hundred Flowers Valley's “Flying Flower Palm” was unleashed in her hands. The palm shadows, like layers upon layers of petals closing in, appeared slow, but each strike sealed off an escape route.

The two attacked from the left and right, their angles perfectly timed.

Ji Mingzhao blocked the front, Su Wantang locked down the retreat.

With the two prodigies attacking from both sides, how would Fang Yuan cope?!

Fang Yuan did not retreat.

Instead, he took a step forward, circulated his inner energy, and then…

Boom!!!

A deafening roar erupted. Hearing the sound, the two paused their attacks for a moment, feeling the world suddenly spin.

Both thought in unison: What is this?!

Meanwhile, the senior members leading the group below the stage looked troubled.

The younger generation on the stage didn't know, but these old fogies were very familiar with it.

The Taoists have two generals, Heng and Ha, whose auras can bewitch the soul. Their medical practitioners, deeply studying the human body, established an internal spirit department. Through collective wisdom, they naturally made progress in this area.

Utilizing the keen senses of the ears, nose, and mouth, the Taoists used the auras of Heng and Ha to interfere with the internal spirit. By analogy, they created an attack method using sound waves as a medium.

Named – The Shocking God Technique!

“Old Han, if I’m not mistaken, that kid used the Shocking God Technique, didn’t he?”

An elder leading a group from the Shennong Sect asked Han Baiqing of Medicine King Valley.

Han Baiqing’s face also showed a look of admiration.

“Truly… a prodigy.”

While the Divine Shock Technique is powerful, it demands a high level of skill from its user. Not only must one possess sufficiently strong internal energy, but also ample mental strength.

At least a cultivator at the Qi Meridian Realm can use it, and even then, they must have achieved some level of spiritual attainment to apply it in actual combat; otherwise, it will result in significant self-inflicted damage.

In other words, Fang Yuan on the stage, capable of harming the two, has already reached the Qi Meridian Realm!

A sixteen-year-old at the Qi Meridian Realm!

The last one this strong was…

“…What incredible luck did Mu Jingxing have, picking up two monstrous talents in a row!”

Looking at the two on the stage, they could only shake their heads helplessly. Although the Qi Meridian Realm doesn't offer a dramatic breakthrough in combat power, for an individual, it's a leap from one to zero. Establishing Qi Meridians connects with heaven and earth, and the nature of a cultivator's internal energy changes according to their understanding—some become more powerful, some more sustained.

However, without exception, it greatly enhances the cultivator's endurance and adjusts the body, pushing it to its limits.

Even though Fang Yuan's cultivation technique didn't significantly boost his combat power, the long and balanced Qi channels provided by the *Nourishing Life Classic* greatly enhanced his stamina, theoretically allowing him to wear down several Qi channels.

Seizing this opening, Fang Yuan decisively attacked the two.

Many experts watched from below, mentally concluding that Su Wantang and Ji Mingzhao's fight was likely over.

Medical practitioners primarily focused on internal cultivation, unlike martial artists who practiced external cultivation and had a higher margin for error in the first three stages.

Fang Yuan lightly stomped his right foot on the bluestone, channeling a powerful force from his Yongquan acupoint into the ground, instantly making him as heavy as a mountain. The rock beneath his feet thudded, and a spiderweb-like crack spread outwards from him.

He shot into Ji Mingzhao's palm like a cannonball.

Ji Mingzhao's pupils shrank to pinpoints.

The instant Fang Yuan's body collided with the range of Ji Mingzhao's palm strike, he made an unbelievable movement—his upper body slightly turned to the side, just enough to avoid the first strike, while simultaneously lowering his left shoulder, using his shoulder blade to take the brunt of the second strike.

Ji Mingzhao felt as if his palm had struck a piece of finely forged steel.

The recoil traveled along his metacarpal bones to his wrist, then up his arm to his shoulder, instantly paralyzing his entire right arm. He gritted his teeth, forcefully gathering his inner energy to stabilize himself. Just as his left hand was about to change its attack, Fang Yuan's counterattack arrived.

Fang Yuan's right fist emerged from his side, slamming into Ji Mingzhao's left arm, which he had been protecting his chest.

Ji Mingzhao was sent flying backward, his feet leaving the ground. He tumbled through the air before barely landing, staggering back seven or eight steps, kneeling on one knee, gasping for breath.

Su Wantang didn't waste the time Ji Mingzhao had bought for her.

The instant Fang Yuan punched Ji Mingzhao away, her palms were already an inch away from Fang Yuan's back.

The Flying Flower Palm of Hundred Flowers Valley wasn't about the sheer force of the palm strike, but rather the hidden energy. The seemingly gentle palm strike was actually layered with internal energy, like a silkworm spinning silk. A single, solid strike would cause the hidden energy to continuously spread within the enemy's body; three layers of hidden energy combined were enough to seal off their meridians.

She didn't hold back, because the person opposite her didn't need her to.

Her palms landed.

Su Wantang felt her palm first encounter a layer of dense, resilient resistance—the protective true energy of the Hunyuan Gong, far more troublesome than any other external martial art. Immediately afterward, she activated the Hundred Flowers Heart Method, pouring in layer upon layer of hidden energy: first to break through defenses, second to penetrate the body, and third to lock the meridians.

However, after these three waves of energy were injected, Su Wantang's expression changed drastically.

After her hidden energy entered Fang Yuan's body, it vanished completely, like a mud ox sinking into the sea, without a trace of feedback.

What she didn't know was that Fang Yuan's "Life" state of mind, while offering no real boost to combat power, granted Fang Yuan himself an extremely powerful ability:

Resistance to all attributes.

Whether it was physical or internal energy attacks, Fang Yuan's resistance was extremely strong. Furthermore, the *Hunyuan Nourishing Life Scripture* itself possessed the restorative effects of balance and harmony, harmonizing Yin and Yang.

The combination of these two elements creates a monster who, while not a body-training martial artist, possesses damage reduction attributes comparable to one.

"Too shallow."

As soon as the words left his mouth, Fang Yuan's back muscles suddenly twitched.

A force several times stronger than what Su Wantang had injected rebounded, flowing through her palms and into her arms.

Su Wantang groaned, thrown back by the impact, landing lightly three zhang away.

She landed on her toes, her posture elegant, but her slightly trembling hands betrayed her condition.

The entire arena was silent.

From the combined attack to their mutual defeat, the entire process happened in the blink of an eye.

Ji Mingzhao, clutching his left arm, rose from the ground, a trickle of blood escaping from the corner of his mouth.

He glanced down at his left hand; his fingers were still trembling slightly, the web between his thumb and forefinger split open, blood trickling down his wrist. He remained silent for a moment, then slowly raised his head, looking at the figure in the center of the arena who exuded immense pressure.

He suddenly smiled.

He knew that continuing was pointless.

He was no match for his opponent.

“I concede.”

He called her by name, his voice slightly hoarse. “You won, Fang Yuan.”

Having said those two sentences, he seemed to have unloaded a tremendous burden.

He turned and walked towards the sidelines. He sat down on a bench and gulped down the water his fellow disciples handed him.

Only Su Wantang and Fang Yuan remained on the field.

Su Wantang stood three zhang away, her long hair soaked with sweat and clinging to her cheeks. She looked at Fang Yuan, her almond-shaped eyes no longer filled with fighting spirit, but rather with scrutiny, the scrutiny of a rare species.

She took a deep breath and slowly lowered her hands.

“I concede too,” she said.

Fang Yuan nodded, offering no polite words of “thank you for your concession,” nor did he feign helping her up.

He turned to Han Baiqing on the sidelines.

Han Baiqing glanced at the young man in the field; his presence, seemingly unassuming, already exuded an air of composure.

"The outcome is decided..."

Han Baiqing looked at the youths on the stage, gathered his strength, and shouted in a deep voice:

"The champion of this tournament is..."

In the silent hall, two words echoed, deafeningly loud:

"Fang Yuan——————!!"

As soon as the two words fell, the entire hall erupted as if a frozen surface had thawed. The Hunyuan Sect group was the most excited.

"He won!"

"One man suppresses his peers!"

"Senior Brother Fang is invincible!"

The audience erupted in cheers; the result had surprised everyone.

Meanwhile, in the stands, the leaders of the various factions watched intently, a senior member of the Thousand Gold Pavilion, holding a cup of tea that had long since gone cold, gazing at the retreating figure of the young man in the arena, his eyes narrowed.

The senior member of the Azure Cloud Medical Lodge put away his paper and pen, and the leaders of his group smiled.

The abbess of the Hundred Flowers Valley watched the young prodigy on the stage with shining eyes.

The expressions of the disciples from each faction were even more varied—some were dumbfounded, some were inexplicably excited, some were ashen-faced, and some had burning gazes.

The losing disciples returned to their respective groups, their faces showing no sorrow; some even wore an inexplicable sense of awe.

But in the center of the arena, Fang Yuan did not leave.

He stood on the cratered bluestone ground and slowly closed his eyes.

In that battle just now, weaving through the attacks of fifteen people, in the instant Ji Mingzhao's palm strike and Su Wantang's hidden force entered his body, he grasped something.

That feeling returned.

The barrier between himself and the world had been torn open in the extreme battle. It wasn't a breakthrough in power, but some more fundamental understanding—his body, his inner energy, his consciousness, had achieved an unprecedented harmony in those few breaths.

That thin veil had been pulled back slightly.

Fang Yuan stood in the center of the training ground, and the aura around him began to change.

No one saw clearly what happened, but some old-timers sensed it.

Something was happening in the air; they vaguely perceived an imperceptible vortex slowly rotating around Fang Yuan.

The morning wind suddenly stopped, and the fluttering of the four flags ceased simultaneously.

On the cliff behind the valley, Sun Sixian, the Valley Master of Medicine King Valley, hadn't gone far. He stopped, glanced back at the direction of the martial arts arena, and sensing the suddenly rising aura, a smile finally appeared on his face.

"Truly exceptional talent. The Hunyuan Sect is really lucky. His medical skills are superb. Should we get him an honorary elder position or something to lure him over? That old codger Mu Jingxing will come after me if he finds out."

Sun Sixian stood for a moment, then finally turned and strode towards the mountain gate, his laughter echoing all the way.

In the martial arts arena, it was almost noon.

Fang Yuan stood in the brightest sunlight, his blue robes gleaming with gold.

After Fang Yuan's victory was announced, Zhao Feixing and Xiao Tian leaped onto the platform and tightly gripped Fang Yuan's neck.

"Hahaha, Junior Brother, you're amazing!"

"I knew you could do it! One against fifteen, you really stole the show in this competition."

The two chattered amongst themselves, while those on the stage curiously observed Fang Yuan. The disciples of the Hunyuan Sect surged onto the stage, lifted Fang Yuan up, and tossed him into the air, shouting in unison:

"Senior Brother Fang! Mighty!

Senior Brother Fang! Mighty!"

Fang Yuan looked at the sky, seemingly both near and far. Although he felt a little strange, the corners of his mouth involuntarily turned up.

The aura of a master he had displayed on the stage was completely destroyed by the cheers of his disciples.

The crowd put him down, and Zhao Feixing still wore a silly grin, a hint of smug satisfaction at Fang Yuan's unparalleled prowess.

Haha, my junior brother is the champion! Our sect is number one!

Fang Yuan steadied himself, his gaze falling on the blue figure below the stage...

Mu Chen didn't rush up with Zhao Feixing and the others; he remained standing below the stage, his blue robe swaying slightly in the wind, exuding a gentle, refined air.

A smile graced Mu Chen's face, more of a satisfaction at Fang Yuan's success than a surprise. He seemed completely unsurprised, confident in Fang Yuan's ability to succeed.

Looking at Mu Chen below the stage, Fang Yuan smiled.

The youthful smile was carefree, radiating youthful vigor.

Fang Yuan looked at Mu Chen, raised his right hand, and shouted,

"Senior Brother! I did it!"

Mu Chen smiled at Fang Yuan.

Fang Yuan gave a somewhat unrestrained, boastful smile.

"Yes!

Senior Brother is proud of you."

Mu Chen said, looking at the young man on the stage.



Chapter 49 The Stepping Stone for the Male Protagonist in a Wuxia Story: The Holy Son 19


"Junior Brother Fang, truly a young hero!"

A cheerful voice came from the side. Ji Mingzhao had changed into clean clothes, his left hand bandaged, but his face showed no sign of defeat or dejection; instead, he appeared relaxed.

Su Wantang followed behind him, her long hair now neatly tied in a bun. Behind them were the elite disciples from various schools participating in the competition.

The other disciples, seeing them approach, subconsciously suppressed their smiles, and the atmosphere became slightly tense.

Ji Mingzhao waved his hand, walked confidently to Fang Yuan, looked him up and down, and shook his head with a laugh: "You rascal, I didn't realize how old you were during the competition, but now that you're up close, how old are you? Sixteen? When I was sixteen, I was still behind my senior brother!"

His tone was self-deprecating, but without a trace of bitterness.

Xue Shaoyan stepped forward and apologized.

"I take back what I said earlier about you being arrogant." Xue Shaoyan bowed, expressing his apology.

Before Fang Yuan could say anything, another sentence was added.

"Although you're still quite infuriating."

"Haha, Young Master Xue, you still look so unwilling."

Ji Mingzhao, seeing Xue Shaoyan's expression, laughed.

Xue Shaoyan curled his lip. They, his peers, didn't know Ji Mingzhao was incredibly arrogant. His attitude was much higher than Fang Yuan's when they first met, but after getting to know him, he had the right to be arrogant.

From childhood to adulthood, he was always the best in both pharmacology and martial arts at Qianjin Pavilion, but after spending time with him, you'd find he was actually a decent person.

He was incredibly aloof and disdainful of strangers, but once you got to know him, he was alright.

He had a chivalrous spirit, bold and generous.

...He could be a friend.

How did Qianjin Pavilion raise such a guy?

The youngest among them, Liu Chuanping, said, looking at Fang Yuan.

Hearing this, the remaining people looked at him with strange expressions.

"What are you talking about!"

Fang Yuan, observing Xue Shaoyan's words and actions, showed no anger, merely returning the greeting to acknowledge his greeting.

He didn't react much to this, and he hadn't sensed any malice from Ji Mingzhao and his group.

Su Wantang stepped forward, her tone much softer than Ji Mingzhao's, yet equally frank: "Thank you for your mercy today, Junior Brother Fang. The hidden force of the Flying Flower Palm struck my body, but your rebound avoided my vital meridians, only injuring my skin and not my foundation. I am truly impressed by your control."

Ji Mingzhao interrupted him: "Alright, alright, stop being so modest. Excessive modesty is just hypocrisy."

Each prominent school of thought has its own Tongji recording its achievements. Besides documenting development, it also records the achievements of some geniuses as role models for future generations.

Like the Medical Immortal, the foremost figure in the Medical School. And Pi Tong, the ancestor of Medicine King Valley, who pioneered many medicines and methods.

Hearing Ji Mingzhao's words, Xue Shaoyan and the others understood.

So that's it!

But thinking about it carefully, it didn't seem wrong. Fang Yuan was exceptionally talented, achieving so much at such a young age. Whether he'd be included in the Tongji was uncertain. But he'd definitely have a place in the history of the Grand Tournament, being the top scholar and martial artist among the sixteen.

Tsk, thinking about it this way, it wasn't so unacceptable.

Anyway, it was only a matter of time; he'd either be defeated this year or next year.

He spoke sincerely, and even the Hunyuan Sect disciples around him raised their heads proudly.

Perhaps their generation could even gain some fame by following Fang Yuan.

They'd have something to brag about to their children for the rest of their lives.

Moreover, to be honest, the medical school had maintained a harmonious internal situation since the Medicine King Valley Conference over a decade ago.

Each faction would present their views and opinions at each conference, engaging in discussions. Although there were occasional disagreements, the overall situation remained stable.

The world was vast enough to accommodate all schools and sects.

Medicine was a subject with many areas where each school was currently short-staffed.

Besides, they knew how they had earned their prestigious degrees.

They had been elevated to that position by their ancestor.

The legendary physician of that time had single-handedly propelled the entire medical school into the ranks of the most prominent medical disciplines in the world, showing everyone just how high the medical school's potential could be.

But there could only be one legendary physician, and even with their best efforts, the younger generation of disciples could never hope to reach his level.

This is why all factions treat true geniuses with great friendliness.

The present era is no longer one where one can achieve anything by working in isolation.

They all understand that for a medical school to solidify its foundation, it needs a continuous stream of top-tier figures capable of holding their own.

Fang Yuan looked into Ji Mingzhao's eyes; the fighting spirit was gone, replaced by a frank appreciation, even a hint of expectation.

"Thank you," Fang Yuan nodded earnestly.

"What are you thanking me for?" Ji Mingzhao was about to slap Fang Yuan on the shoulder, but stopped abruptly with a wave of his hand.

The medicine that has just been applied cannot be touched.

"Alright, I'm going to apply my medicine now. You guys enjoy your celebration. Come find me tonight if you're free... for some herbal tea. Our Qianjin Pavilion's Qingxin Tea is absolutely amazing."

He turned and took a few steps, then turned back and added, "By the way, Fang Yuan, there's a big conference coming up at the herb garden behind Medicine King Valley. Want to go check it out sometime?"

Ji Mingzhao's implication was to ease tensions and simultaneously recruit Fang Yuan into their group.

Sure enough, the fragrance of flowers attracts butterflies.

Having achieved his goal, Fang Yuan readily agreed.

Ji Mingzhao left satisfied. Su Wantang nodded slightly to Fang Yuan and also turned to leave.

As soon as the two left, another group of people surrounded them.

"Nephew Fang, you are truly remarkable at such a young age. In my sixty-odd years, this is the first time I've seen someone reach the Qi Meridian Realm at sixteen," said the leader of the Shennong Sect, an elderly man with white hair and beard, stroking his beard with a smile. "The Hunyuan Sect has a worthy successor; congratulations!"

Several Shennong Sect disciples echoed this sentiment, their tone tinged with admiration.

Nephew Fang, please don't refuse. Come visit us anytime; the entire sect will certainly prepare a grand welcome."

Fang Yuan glanced at Mu Chen behind him, who stood with his arms crossed, smiling broadly at him.

(The implication being: Junior Brother, you can't escape this. Prepare to face it.)

Before Fang Yuan could even exchange pleasantries, the elder patted his hand and said in a low voice, "Our sect leader said that if you ever wish to travel, nephew, the position of honorary elder of the sect is always at your disposal."

The words weren't spoken loudly, but many of the surrounding cultivators, with sharp ears and eyes, heard them immediately.

Han Baiqing, who had appeared out of nowhere, slapped the elder's hand away with displeasure. "Old Chen, poaching people right in front of me?"

Elder Chen rubbed his nose, chuckled twice, and didn't argue.

Han Baiqing turned to Fang Yuan, his expression full of admiration. He handed him a golden token engraved with a hundred herbs and a bottle of pills, then said in a complicated tone:

"These are your rewards for winning first place this time. From now on, we won't leave such a prodigy as you unrewarded. You can freely enter the first three floors of the valley's library. This is the valley master's order."

Fang Yuan was slightly taken aback. While the three-story library of Medicine King Valley wasn't considered a core secret repository, the medical classics and annotations it contained were invaluable treasures.

This gift was undeniably substantial.

"Thank you, Senior Han, thank you for your kindness, Valley Master," Fang Yuan said solemnly, bowing.

Han Baiqing nodded, his gaze lingering on him for a moment, lost in thought, before turning and leaving.

“Nephew Fang,” Abbess Yilin said with a smile, her tone so warm that Sun Dazhu, standing nearby, perked up his ears. “This humble nun has a question for you.”

Fang Yuan had a good impression of this abbess—during their exchange, Su Wantang's attacks, though fierce, were all upright and honorable; her internal energy, though penetrating the body, only affected the meridians without harming the internal organs, demonstrating the high moral character of Hundred Flowers Valley. “Please speak, Abbess.”

Fang Yuan's smile froze.

Oh dear, why didn't I think of that! I also have several unmarried granddaughters/disciples.

Fang Yuan really did it!

Number one in both literature and martial arts!

Our Hunyuan Sect has produced a dragon!



Chapter 50 The Stepping Stone for the Male Protagonist of a Wuxia Story: The Holy Son 20


"Father!"

"Master, Ling is right. Judging by the timing, it should be about the right time. Senior brother should have news by now."

Li Huaisu walked past, first bowing to Mu Jingxing, and then spoke. She managed many of the household items and was extremely sensitive to time.

Judging by the time, it should be around these next few days.

"First place?! Junior brother got first place?!"

The champion, a title specifically bestowed upon those who achieved first place in both literary and martial arts at the Medicine King Valley Tournament, was a title held by a master who had been renowned throughout the land for decades.

It carries immense weight.

Realizing this, Mu Ling was overjoyed, clutching the letter and spinning around the room, muttering, “Junior Brother is amazing!” “Champion, oh champion!” She nearly bumped into the doorframe when Li Huaisu pulled her back.
