Hearing System 120's voice, Fang Yuan's lowered face slightly curved upwards, but he still told System 120 that everything was proceeding as planned.

Xue Shaoyan looked at the rescued Fang Yuan, his expression stiff, muttering incessantly, "Why, why, even the heavens favor you!!"

Looking at the white bird, Xue Shaoyan's face twisted in rage.

Fang Yuan stumbled to his feet, raising his head, his eyes fixed on him.

"Why? Why did you do this!"

Fang Yuan didn't understand why Xue Shaoyan would do this. During the conferences over the past few days, they had gained a general understanding of him: he came from a wealthy family, possessed outstanding talent, and was considered a future heir or an important elder in their sect.

Why would someone like that use a curse on a group of ordinary people!

Upon hearing this, Xue Shaoyan tilted his head, a chilling smile spreading across his pale face.

"Didn't I tell you? Junior Brother Fang, you're so outstanding, how could a prodigy like you understand the feelings of a mortal like me!"

Fang Yuan looked at him incredulously, all for this reason.

"Die, Junior Brother Fang!"

With that, Xue Shaoyan charged at Fang Yuan, his face expressionless, but coupled with his bloodless appearance, he looked like a demon crawling out of the deepest hell, sending shivers down one's spine.

Fang Yuan stumbled and tried to dodge, but his internal energy was sealed. The poison he'd been given wasn't just a single substance; he felt dizzy and his body was numb.

At this moment, Fang Yuan was like a drugged piglet, waiting for Xue Shaoyan's attack to strike and die. But at this critical moment, the white bird struck again, swooping down from the sky to pierce Xue Shaoyan.

A white bird swooped down, its sharp beak flashing like a white lightning bolt, aiming straight for Xue Shaoyan's face. Xue Shaoyan instinctively turned his head, the beak grazing his forehead, leaving a stray hair and a shallow bloodstain.

Xue Shaoyan countered with a powerful palm strike, the force of the blow forcing the white bird back several feet.

But the white bird was extremely agile. With a mid-air turn, it swooped down again, its wings whipping up fine wind blades that hissed through the air. Xue Shaoyan had to halt his charge towards Fang Yuan and turn to fight the feathered beast that had appeared out of nowhere.

Fang Yuan seized the opportunity to stagger back, leaning against a thick tree trunk. He pulled a pill from his pocket, swallowed it, closed his eyes, and focused his mind, beginning to circulate his internal energy.

Hmm, this one seems to have a little too little honey.

Fang Yuan sat cross-legged, appearing to be racing against time, but inwardly he was communicating with System 120.

"Can I win?"

"Yes, the opponent's combat power isn't very strong."

System 120 replied.

Don't be fooled by this plump, white bird. As a projection of System 120's world consciousness, although limited to this bird, its combat power shouldn't be underestimated.

This bird's original form is a mythical beast from the snowy mountains of the northern world. Even in its youth, it could tear apart tigers and leopards with its bare hands. Some even say its ancestors had extremely long lifespans and formidable fighting power, and still reside in the snowy mountains today.

It is regarded as a totem by some tribes; calling it a divine beast wouldn't be an exaggeration.

This seemingly adorable but somewhat dim-witted bird boasts maxed-out racial stats and personality, and possesses the operational capabilities of System 120.

It can be said to be a fat bird with extraordinary talent!

Although currently in its very infancy, it's more than capable of dealing with Xue Shaoyan, who is completely out of his mind and only possesses brute strength.

System 120 dodged the opponent's attack, used a peck while the opponent controlled the field, and then dodged again with a sidestep. Xue Shaoyan was about to attack Fang Yuan, so System 120 swooped down again to interfere.

It deeply understood the essence of the eight-character mantra: "When the enemy advances, I retreat; when the enemy is exhausted, I harass." Its attacks were executed with remarkable skill and strategy.

The black-bellied man watching System 120 and Xue Shaoyan's battle from a short distance away was also dumbfounded.

"Where did this rare and exotic beast come from?"

Even villains aren't simple characters. The black-robed man, looking at System 120 protecting Fang Yuan, secretly clicked his tongue in amazement. This beast's attacks and retreats were surprisingly methodical?

Looking at Fang Yuan, who was only a few feet away from Xue Shaoyan, he couldn't help but wonder if this guy truly had great fortune?

This can't drag on any longer! The black-robed man picked up the bone whistle again, channeling his inner energy into it, and propelled it once more.

Several dark figures not far away, startled by the sound, quickened their pace.

To Fang Yuan's left, a turquoise snake, its body a finger's width, slithered out from beside him, hissing and flicking its tongue, its eyes gleaming with bloodlust.

Although Fang Yuan appeared to be cross-legged, adjusting his state, his inner energy chaotic, he was actually secretly observing the situation.

His current state was merely a concealed form for adjusting his state; the "Primordial Chaos, Formless and Clear Qi" technique was no joke.

He already harbored suspicions about Xue Shaoyan, so naturally he wouldn't eat all the food Xue Shaoyan brought.

Pretending to be poisoned was a ploy to lure the mastermind behind the scenes. He appeared to be recuperating cross-legged, but in reality, he was waiting for the mastermind to appear or for System 120 to give way, ready to strike at any moment.

The snake, having reached Fang Yuan's side, suddenly exerted its strength, baring its fangs with a speed and explosive power unlike any other snake of its kind, and viciously bit at Fang Yuan.

Whoosh!

Fang Yuan was prepared. He opened his eyes, and with a quick backhand, he grabbed the snake's head in his hand.

The snake's muscles were incredibly strong. Even with its head held, it didn't give up, arching its body and whipping its tail with a cracking sound.

Fang Yuan was struck hard on the arm by the snake's tail, making a loud sound. For Fang Yuan, a numerical monster possessing the power of "life" and cultivating the *Hun Yuan Yang Sheng Jing* (a martial arts manual), this attack was nothing more than a tickle. However, for some women with little cultivation, it would probably mean a trip to the clinic afterwards.

Fang Yuan tightened his grip, and the green snake's head cracked in his palm. The snake's body twitched a few times before drooping limply. He casually tossed the snake carcass aside, his gaze sweeping around. Rustling sounds continued from the grass; several brightly colored venomous snakes had emerged from different directions, their triangular heads slightly raised, their tongues flicking, surrounding him.

He took out a snake-repelling medicine packet from his pocket, activated his inner energy, and the powder turned into a cloud of smoke. However, the snakes only paused for a moment, their eyes gleaming even more fiercely, and they continued to approach.



Chapter 55 The Stepping Stone for the Male Protagonist of a Wuxia Story: The Holy Son 25


Fang Yuan's expression remained unchanged, but he thought to himself,

This snake was controlled by Gu magic; ordinary snake repellent was indeed useless.

Fang Yuan casually tossed aside the empty medicine packet and looked up at the dark, dense forest in the distance.

He had heard that bone whistle clearly just now.

"One hundred and twenty paces, southwest, where the pines and cypresses intertwine," Fang Yuan murmured to himself. "A long, drawn-out aura; it's a master."

The location was clear; it was time.

“120,” his voice echoed in his mind, “Switch positions.”

“Understood!”

The white bird, locked in combat with Xue Shaoyan, let out a clear cry upon hearing the call. Its wings flapped suddenly, unleashing several wind blades that forced Xue Shaoyan back two steps. Then, it transformed into a white blur, swooping directly towards Fang Yuan.

Freed from the white bird's restraint, Xue Shaoyan staggered. His bloodshot eyes locked onto Fang Yuan, a twisted grin spreading across his lips. He let out a muffled growl, pushing off with his feet, lunging at Fang Yuan like a wild beast out of control.

Fang Yuan did not retreat.

Instead, he met him head-on.

His steps were steady, his robes fluttering, the breathing techniques of the Hunyuan lineage already circulating within his body. The sealed internal energy had begun to loosen when the pill had entered his stomach, and now, like spring ice melting, it gently and irresistibly replenished his meridians.

“Senior Brother Xue,” Fang Yuan said softly, his gaze calm to the point of pity, “I’m sorry to have kept you waiting.”

His figure left a blur in the night, passing directly beside Xue Shaoyan.

Li Aobin, hidden in the shadows, witnessed everything, a cold smile curling at the corner of his lips. He assumed Fang Yuan was at his limit, a cornered dog making a last-ditch effort.

“What a pity,” Li Aobin sighed inwardly, a morbid excitement gleaming in his eyes, “The number one genius of the Yao family will perish in this desolate wilderness today.”

He licked his dry lips, his fingers already pressed against the Gu pouch at his waist, waiting to launch a sneak attack while Fang Yuan was engaged in combat with Xue Shaoyan.

Speaking of this, Li Aobin also felt a sense of pent-up resentment.

He and Wu Yao hadn’t come to this area near Qing Shi Town to cause trouble.

Although the Five Gu Sect wasn't a prestigious sect, its survival in the martial world was due to its discerning eye for who to mess with. The two men had spent days lurking in the mountains, hoping to capture a rare five-colored Gu worm. Just when they were about to succeed, Wu Yao, that scoundrel, suffered a stroke during his cultivation, causing his internal Gu worm to malfunction and spread. By the time they discovered it, it had already infected the people of Qing Shi Town.

Li Aobin still seethes with rage at the thought of it.

They knew, of course, that Qing Shi Town was only a three-day journey from Medicine King Valley, and the Yao family was not to be trifled with. If they attracted the Yao family's attention, they would be in deep trouble.

The two men originally intended to quickly retrieve the Gu worm and quietly end the matter, but just as they emerged from the mountains, they stumbled upon Xue Shaoyan and several disciples investigating the town.

If this kid continued his investigation and discovered the Gu worm, and the news reached the Yao family, the two men would be doomed.

Even more coincidentally, Xue Shaoyan contracted the Gu worm while investigating the source of the illness. Although his cultivation technique provided some resistance to Gu worms, he was still young and emotionally unstable, allowing the Gu worms to exploit his weaknesses, and his emotions gradually became manipulated.

Li Aobin and Wu Yao exchanged a glance, immediately hatching a wicked plan.

They would control Xue Shaoyan, frame the incident as a plague, then eliminate the other sect disciples, destroying the evidence and leaving no witnesses.

Afterwards, the two would flee far away; how could they be caught in the vast sea of ​​people?

This was a foolproof plan.

But then Fang Yuan appeared out of nowhere.

Others might not notice, but Li Aobin knew that the most knowledgeable about Gu techniques within the Yao family was the usually low-profile Hunyuan Sect.

Over the years, people had been secretly analyzing the Gu techniques of various sects; if the people from Qingyun Medicine Pavilion hadn't noticed anything amiss, how could the Hunyuan Sect not?

Even more deadly was that these new disciples clearly recognized Xue Shaoyan.

Li Aobin felt a chill run down his spine.

If he and Wu Yao were to flee, the uncontrolled Gu worm within Xue Shaoyan's body would either destroy his meridians or leave him utterly destroyed. Once the Yao family arrived and traced the entire affair, the two of them would face the relentless pursuit of the entire Yao family.

That was no joke.

But staying meant certain death as well. Li Aobin narrowed his eyes, sizing up Mu Chen. He had a bad feeling about that kid, and the handsome young man beside him was rumored to be the Yao family's top genius of this generation, with so many fellow disciples. If they were to encounter him, they wouldn't survive either.

If either of them escaped, they would be hunted to the ends of the earth.

Just as the two were caught in this dilemma, Fang Yuan and Mu Chen's conversation reached their ears—they felt the matter couldn't be resolved and wanted to go to Medicine King Valley to ask a senior to intervene.

Li Aobin and Wu Yao exchanged a glance, cold sweat pouring down their backs.

They couldn't wait any longer.

The two immediately decided: go all the way. Li Aobin would control Xue Shaoyan, poison Fang Yuan who remained in charge, and then have Xue Shaoyan personally kill him. Judging from their conversation, the two seemed to have some old grudges; even if suspicion arose, they would have long since parted ways.

Meanwhile, Wu Yao would intercept Mu Chen, who was going to seek help, and then quietly dispose of the seriously ill patients in the village, finally letting the wandering Zi Gu commit suicide.

With Zi Gu dead, there would be no way to prove anything. There were so many people in the world capable of such things; even if they were investigated, who would know who it was?

Li Aobin pulled himself back to the battlefield. Xue Shaoyan was frantically charging towards Fang Yuan, his martial arts foundation still intact, his attacks ruthless and fierce, completely devoid of his former gentleness.

And Fang Yuan, surprisingly, didn't dodge or evade, charging straight at him.

Young people are young, impatient, knowing they're poisoned but still acting rashly. He had already planned his next move, just waiting for Fang Yuan to make a mistake.

However, the next instant, his smile froze on his face.

In the instant Fang Yuan's figure crossed paths with Xue Shaoyan, he flicked his wrist as easily as brushing away a fallen leaf, sending Xue Shaoyan flying backward, crashing heavily into a pine tree, sliding limply to the ground, unconscious.

The movement was effortless, as if tossing aside a rag doll.

Immediately afterward, Fang Yuan's figure didn't pause for a moment, like an arrow released from a bow, heading straight for Li Aobin's hiding place.

His direction was precise, without any deviation.

His eyes shone astonishingly bright in the night, where was the confusion caused by poisoning?

Li Aobin's pupils constricted sharply, a thought flashing through his mind like a bucket of cold water poured over his head.

"This kid's acting!"

From beginning to end, Fang Yuan had been acting.

Li Aobin had no time to think. He pushed off the ground with both legs, his figure retreating rapidly.

As a Gu Master, seventy percent of his skills lay in controlling Gu worms; close combat had never been his forte. He needed distance, even just three or five zhang (approximately 10-15 meters). As long as he could create space, he had dozens of Gu worms at his disposal.

However, Fang Yuan didn't give him that chance.

"Eight Steps in a Row!"

Fang Yuan shouted, his footwork unfolding. His inner energy surged, his robes fluttering, his figure flashing repeatedly in the night, so fast it almost left afterimages. In the blink of an eye, the distance between the two was compressed to less than three zhang (approximately 10 meters).

Veins bulged on Li Aobin's forehead. In haste, he grabbed several Gu worms from his Gu pouch at his waist and tossed them out.

The Gu worms exploded in mid-air, creating a cloud of gray mist that transformed into several black streaks of light shooting towards Fang Yuan's face.

Fang Yuan didn't even blink. With a flick of his robe, a powerful surge of internal energy swept out, sweeping the Gu worms and the gray mist aside.

The Gu worms crashed into the tree trunk, hissing and corroding, instantly charring the trunk black.

Li Aobin's pupils constricted sharply. He tried to retreat again, but it was too late.

Fang Yuan took a step in front of him, his right fist, imbued with surging internal energy, striking Li Aobin's chest without any flourish.

One punch.

A dull thud accompanied the cracking sound of bones shattering. Li Aobin was sent flying like a kite with a broken string, spitting out blood and carving a furrow several meters long into the ground, raising a cloud of dust.

Fang Yuan stopped, his brow furrowing slightly as he looked at Li Aobin, who lay motionless on the ground, a flicker of doubt in his eyes.

Is it over just like that?

No.

The dust gradually settled, and Li Aobin struggled to his feet. A dent was clearly visible in his chest, and blood still clung to the corner of his mouth, but his eyes gleamed with a crazed ferocity.

"Good, good..." Li Aobin gasped, each word laced with the metallic taste of blood, "As expected of the Yao family's number one genius... I underestimated you..."

That was a heavy punch...

Li Aobin frantically considered what method could possibly help him escape this predicament.

Golden Body Gu, Swift Movement Gu, no... none of them would work.

Li Aobin hadn't expected that what he thought was the second level, his opponent was actually on the fourth.

As a Xiantian Realm cultivator, even as a Gu Master, his Zhou Tian Sensing allowed him to kill anyone with ordinary Qi channels in a purely physical fight.

But when Fang Yuan truly unleashed his full power, Li Aobin felt a chill run down his spine.

Especially after being severely injured.

"This won't do. If this continues, the Gu worms in my body will turn on me."

"I'll risk it!"

He bit his tongue hard, spitting a mouthful of blood into his palm. Immediately afterward, several jet-black Gu worms crawled out from under his robes, burrowing into his wound and disappearing into his body.

Golden Body Gu, Mighty Gu, Void Hunting Gu…

Li Aobin's body began to tremble violently. His skin visibly turned grayish-white, then a metallic sheen. The veins beneath his skin bulged, his muscles swelled, and his body grew noticeably taller.

Fang Yuan's eyes sharpened. Without hesitation, he rushed forward, leaping into the air and delivering a powerful flying kick to Li Aobin's chest, which was undergoing its transformation.

Another muffled thud followed, and Li Aobin was sent flying again, crashing into several small trees and kicking up a cloud of dust.

But this time, Fang Yuan's brows furrowed even more deeply.

From within the dust, a burly, gray figure slowly rose. Its silhouette was even more ferocious than before, and its breath carried a pungent, fishy stench. A pair of eyes, no longer recognizable as human, stared intently at Fang Yuan through the smoke and dust.

"Die... brat..."

The voice was hoarse, like a broken gong.
